                         <h3 class="zi"><a href="./114852685785546775114" class="ob tv Ub Hf" oid="114852685785546775114"><span dir="ltr">OpenID Foundation</span>‏</a></h3>
                         <span class="uG Ve"><span role="button" class="d-s Vt Hm dk Q9" title="مشاركة التفاصيل" tabindex="0" jsname="lUFH9b" aria-haspopup="true">تمت المشاركة بشكل عام</span> &nbsp;-&nbsp; <span class="uv PL"><a href="+openid/posts/eUQzr66SYCA" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="o-U-s FI Rg" style="display:none">2012-03-08</a></span></span>

                          </div>
                          <div class="Ct" dir="ltr">
                           The OIDF Account Chooser working group is now very close to launching the first version of a central Account Chooser service. On March 22nd we are holding a meeting of the working group in Silicon Valley, and others are invited to participate, including by watching a live video of the event.﻿
